# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

## Summary

I've identified and documented the complete datasource query path in Grafana, which includes **32 Go source files** organized across multiple architectural layers:

### Key Layers Identified:

1. **HTTP Request Handler** - `pkg/api/ds_query.go` (QueryMetricsV2)
2. **Query Service Orchestration** - `pkg/services/query/query.go` (ServiceImpl with query parsing, datasource routing, and concurrent execution)
3. **Plugin Context Provider** - `pkg/services/pluginsintegration/plugincontext/provider.go` (builds plugin contexts with datasource settings)
4. **Plugin Client Dispatcher** - `pkg/plugins/manager/client/client.go` (routes to registered plugins)
5. **Plugin Implementation** - `pkg/plugins/plugins.go` (plugin wrapper and dispatcher)
6. **Datasource Handlers** - 11+ datasource implementations (Loki, Tempo, Jaeger, Zipkin, PostgreSQL, MySQL, Graphite, Parca, Testdata, etc.)
7. **Expression Service** - `pkg/expr/service.go` and `pkg/expr/transform.go` (handles server-side expressions)
8. **Middleware Layer** - Caching, tracing, and logging middleware

### The Query Path Flow:
```
HTTP Request → Query Service → Plugin Context → Plugin Client → Datasource Handler → Response Aggregation
```

Overview\\nThe datasource plugin query path in Grafana follows a multi-layered architecture that handles query requests, dispatches them to appropriate plugins, and returns aggregated responses. The flow consists of HTTP request handling, query service orchestration, plugin context management, plugin dispatch, and response transformation.\\n\\n### HTTP Request Handler Layer\\n**File: `pkg/api/ds_query.go`**\\n- **QueryMetricsV2**: Main HTTP handler for POST `/api/ds/query` endpoint that receives metric query requests\\n- Validates incoming request (MetricRequest DTO) with optional time handling flag\\n- Calls query service with proper context (user, cache settings, request details)\\n- **toJsonStreamingResponse**: Transforms QueryDataResponse to HTTP response with status codes\\n- Handles error responses and downstream status attribution\\n\\n### Query Service Orchestration\\n**File: `pkg/services/query/query.go`**\\n- **ServiceImpl**: Core query orchestration service implementing the Service interface\\n  - **QueryData/QueryDataNew**: Entry points for query execution with optional per-query time range support\\n  - **parseMetricRequest**: Parses incoming requests and groups queries by datasource UID\\n    - Validates datasources exist and user has access\\n    - Handles expression datasources (e.g., \\\"__expr__\\\") vs regular datasources\\n    - Extracts time ranges, intervals, max data points, and query types\\n  - **handleQuerySingleDatasource**: Processes queries for a single datasource\\n    - Creates backend.QueryDataRequest with parsed queries\\n    - Builds plugin context using pluginContextProvider\\n    - Routes to plugin client or query-service flow based on feature toggles\\n  - **handleExpressions**: Processes expression queries by building expression request objects\\n  - **executeConcurrentQueries**: Executes queries to multiple datasources in parallel\\n  - **getDataSourceFromQuery**: Resolves datasources from query, handling special types (expressions, Grafana DS)\\n\\n### Plugin Context Provider\\n**File: `pkg/services/pluginsintegration/plugincontext/provider.go`**\\n- **Provider**: Creates and manages backend.PluginContext for datasource plugins\\n- **GetWithDataSource**: Builds plugin context containing:\\n  - Plugin ID and version\\n  - Datasource instance settings (name, UID, type, configuration)\\n  - User identity and organization\\n  - Grafana configuration and feature flags\\n\\n### Plugin Client (Dispatcher)\\n**File: `pkg/plugins/manager/client/client.go`**\\n- **Service**: Implements plugins.Client interface for plugin dispatch\\n- **QueryData**: Routes queries to registered plugins\\n  - Resolves plugin from registry using plugin ID and version\\n  - Invokes plugin's QueryData method\\n  - Handles errors (grpc status, context cancellation, plugin unavailability)\\n  - Sets RefID on returned frames if not already set\\n  - Returns QueryDataResponse with aggregated results\\n\\n### Plugin Implementation Layer\\n**File: `pkg/plugins/plugins.go`**\\n- **Plugin**: Represents a backend plugin implementation\\n  - Implements backend.QueryDataHandler interface\\n  - **QueryData**: Dispatches to actual plugin client implementation (gRPC or process-based)\\n  - Manages plugin lifecycle and client connection\\n\\n### Datasource-Specific Query Handlers\\nEach datasource plugin implements the backend.QueryDataHandler interface:\\n- **Loki** (`pkg/tsdb/loki/loki.go`): Time series and log querying with LogQL support\\n- **Tempo** (`pkg/tsdb/tempo/tempo.go`): Trace querying with trace search and span search\\n- **Jaeger** (`pkg/tsdb/jaeger/jaeger.go`): Jaeger trace backend support\\n- **Zipkin** (`pkg/tsdb/zipkin/zipkin.go`): Zipkin trace backend support\\n- **Graphite** (`pkg/tsdb/graphite/graphite.go`): Graphite metric querying\\n- **Parca** (`pkg/tsdb/parca/plugin.go`, `pkg/tsdb/parca/service.go`): Profiling data support\\n- **PostgreSQL** (`pkg/tsdb/grafana-postgresql-datasource/postgres_service.go`): SQL querying via pgx/sql drivers\\n- **MySQL** (`pkg/tsdb/mysql/mysql_service.go`): SQL querying via MySQL driver\\n- **Testdata** (`pkg/tsdb/grafana-testdata-datasource/testdata.go`): Testing and demo data\\n- **Grafana DS** (`pkg/tsdb/grafanads/grafana.go`): Internal datasource queries\\n\\nEach service:\\n- Implements backend.QueryDataHandler interface\\n- Receives backend.QueryDataRequest with parsed queries\\n- Returns backend.QueryDataResponse with frames and error details\\n- Handles datasource-specific transformations and error handling\\n\\n### Expression Service (Query Transformation)\\n**File: `pkg/expr/service.go`** and **`pkg/expr/transform.go`**\\n- **Service**: Handles server-side expressions and transformations\\n- **TransformData**: Processes expression requests\\n  - Builds expression pipeline from request\\n  - Executes pipeline with data from datasource queries\\n  - Returns aggregated response\\n- **ExecutePipeline**: Runs expression nodes and transforms data\\n- **ResultConverter** (`pkg/expr/converter.go`): Converts datasource-specific responses to standardized format\\n\\n### Response Transformation\\n- **backend.NewQueryDataResponse()**: Creates standard response container\\n- **backend.DataResponse**: Contains frames (data.Frame), error details, and metadata\\n- Response aggregation in query service combines responses from multiple datasources\\n- Status code determination based on presence of errors in responses\\n\\n### Query Registry and API Server Integration\\n**File: `pkg/registry/apis/query/query.go`**\\n- Implements Kubernetes-style query API endpoint\\n- Integrates with datasource API servers\\n- Routes queries through new query service architecture\\n\\n**File: `pkg/registry/apis/datasource/register.go`**\\n- Builds datasource API endpoints\\n- Manages datasource-specific querying through API servers\\n\\n### Middleware and Instrumentation\\n- **Caching Middleware** (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/clientmiddleware/caching_middleware.go`): Query result caching\\n- **Tracing Middleware** (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/clientmiddleware/tracing_middleware.go`): OpenTelemetry tracing\\n- **Contextual Logger Middleware** (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/clientmiddleware/contextual_logger_middleware.go`): Context-aware logging\\n\\n### Request Flow Summary\\n1. HTTP request arrives at `/api/ds/query` endpoint (QueryMetricsV2)\\n2. Query service parses MetricRequest and groups queries by datasource\\n3. For single datasource: CreatePluginContext \u2192 PluginClient.QueryData \u2192 Plugin.QueryData\\n4. For multiple datasources: Execute concurrently with error recovery\\n5. For expressions: Build expression request \u2192 ExprService.TransformData \u2192 ResultConverter\\n6. Aggregate responses and return as JSON with appropriate HTTP status code\\n7. Middleware layers handle caching, tracing, and logging at plugin client level\"\n}\n",

\"github.com/sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec\", \"path\": \"pkg/api/ds_query.go\", \"symbol\": \"toJsonStreamingResponse\"}\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"## Grafana Datasource Plugin Query Architecture\\n\\n### Overview\\nThe datasource plugin query path in Grafana follows a multi-layered architecture that handles query requests, dispatches them to appropriate plugins, and returns aggregated responses. The flow consists of HTTP request handling, query service orchestration, plugin context management, plugin dispatch, and response transformation.\\n\\n### HTTP Request Handler Layer\\n**File: `pkg/api/ds_query.go`**\\n- **QueryMetricsV2**: Main HTTP handler for POST `/api/ds/query` endpoint that receives metric query requests\\n- Validates incoming request (MetricRequest DTO) with optional time handling flag\\n- Calls query service with proper context (user, cache settings, request details)\\n- **toJsonStreamingResponse**: Transforms QueryDataResponse to HTTP response with status codes\\n- Handles error responses and downstream status attribution\\n\\n### Query Service Orchestration\\n**File: `pkg/services/query/query.go`**\\n- **ServiceImpl**: Core query orchestration service implementing the Service interface\\n  - **QueryData/QueryDataNew**: Entry points for query execution with optional per-query time range support\\n  - **parseMetricRequest**: Parses incoming requests and groups queries by datasource UID\\n    - Validates datasources exist and user has access\\n    - Handles expression datasources (e.g., \\\"__expr__\\\") vs regular datasources\\n    - Extracts time ranges, intervals, max data points, and query types\\n  - **handleQuerySingleDatasource**: Processes queries for a single datasource\\n    - Creates backend.QueryDataRequest with parsed queries\\n    - Builds plugin context using pluginContextProvider\\n    - Routes to plugin client or query-service flow based on feature toggles\\n  - **handleExpressions**: Processes expression queries by building expression request objects\\n  - **executeConcurrentQueries**: Executes queries to multiple datasources in parallel\\n  - **getDataSourceFromQuery**: Resolves datasources from query, handling special types (expressions, Grafana DS)\\n\\n### Plugin Context Provider\\n**File: `pkg/services/pluginsintegration/plugincontext/provider.go`**\\n- **Provider**: Creates and manages backend.PluginContext for datasource plugins\\n- **GetWithDataSource**: Builds plugin context containing:\\n  - Plugin ID and version\\n  - Datasource instance settings (name, UID, type, configuration)\\n  - User identity and organization\\n  - Grafana configuration and feature flags\\n\\n### Plugin Client (Dispatcher)\\n**File: `pkg/plugins/manager/client/client.go`**\\n- **Service**: Implements plugins.Client interface for plugin dispatch\\n- **QueryData**: Routes queries to registered plugins\\n  - Resolves plugin from registry using plugin ID and version\\n  - Invokes plugin's QueryData method\\n  - Handles errors (grpc status, context cancellation, plugin unavailability)\\n  - Sets RefID on returned frames if not already set\\n  - Returns QueryDataResponse with aggregated results\\n\\n### Plugin Implementation Layer\\n**File: `pkg/plugins/plugins.go`**\\n- **Plugin**: Represents a backend plugin implementation\\n  - Implements backend.QueryDataHandler interface\\n  - **QueryData**: Dispatches to actual plugin client implementation (gRPC or process-based)\\n  - Manages plugin lifecycle and client connection\\n\\n### Datasource-Specific Query Handlers\\nEach datasource plugin implements the backend.QueryDataHandler interface:\\n- **Loki** (`pkg/tsdb/loki/loki.go`): Time series and log querying with LogQL support\\n- **Tempo** (`pkg/tsdb/tempo/tempo.go`): Trace querying with trace search and span search\\n- **Jaeger** (`pkg/tsdb/jaeger/jaeger.go`): Jaeger trace backend support\\n- **Zipkin** (`pkg/tsdb/zipkin/zipkin.go`): Zipkin trace backend support\\n- **Graphite** (`pkg/tsdb/graphite/graphite.go`): Graphite metric querying\\n- **Parca** (`pkg/tsdb/parca/plugin.go`, `pkg/tsdb/parca/service.go`): Profiling data support\\n- **PostgreSQL** (`pkg/tsdb/grafana-postgresql-datasource/postgres_service.go`): SQL querying via pgx/sql drivers\\n- **MySQL** (`pkg/tsdb/mysql/mysql_service.go`): SQL querying via MySQL driver\\n- **Testdata** (`pkg/tsdb/grafana-testdata-datasource/testdata.go`): Testing and demo data\\n- **Grafana DS** (`pkg/tsdb/grafanads/grafana.go`): Internal datasource queries\\n\\nEach service:\\n- Implements backend.QueryDataHandler interface\\n- Receives backend.QueryDataRequest with parsed queries\\n- Returns backend.QueryDataResponse with frames and error details\\n- Handles datasource-specific transformations and error handling\\n\\n### Expression Service (Query Transformation)\\n**File: `pkg/expr/service.go`** and **`pkg/expr/transform.go`**\\n- **Service**: Handles server-side expressions and transformations\\n- **TransformData**: Processes expression requests\\n  - Builds expression pipeline from request\\n  - Executes pipeline with data from datasource queries\\n  - Returns aggregated response\\n- **ExecutePipeline**: Runs expression nodes and transforms data\\n- **ResultConverter** (`pkg/expr/converter.go`): Converts datasource-specific responses to standardized format\\n\\n### Response Transformation\\n- **backend.NewQueryDataResponse()**: Creates standard response container\\n- **backend.DataResponse**: Contains frames (data.Frame), error details, and metadata\\n- Response aggregation in query service combines responses from multiple datasources\\n- Status code determination based on presence of errors in responses\\n\\n### Query Registry and API Server Integration\\n**File: `pkg/registry/apis/query/query.go`**\\n- Implements Kubernetes-style query API endpoint\\n- Integrates with datasource API servers\\n- Routes queries through new query service architecture\\n\\n**File: `pkg/registry/apis/datasource/register.go`**\\n- Builds datasource API endpoints\\n- Manages datasource-specific querying through API servers\\n\\n### Middleware and Instrumentation\\n- **Caching Middleware** (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/clientmiddleware/caching_middleware.go`): Query result caching\\n- **Tracing Middleware** (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/clientmiddleware/tracing_middleware.go`): OpenTelemetry tracing\\n- **Contextual Logger Middleware** (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/clientmiddleware/contextual_logger_middleware.go`): Context-aware logging\\n\\n### Request Flow Summary\\n1. HTTP request arrives at `/api/ds/query` endpoint (QueryMetricsV2)\\n2. Query service parses MetricRequest and groups queries by datasource\\n3. For single datasource: CreatePluginContext \u2192 PluginClient.QueryData \u2192 Plugin.QueryData\\n4. For multiple datasources: Execute concurrently with error recovery\\n5. For expressions: Build expression request \u2192 ExprService.TransformData \u2192 ResultConverter\\n6. Aggregate responses and return as JSON with appropriate HTTP status code\\n7. Middleware layers handle caching, tracing, and logging at plugin client level\"\n}\n",
